msg:Most are quite satisfied. It would be better if a few small details could be improved.

Let me first talk about a few points that I am satisfied with:
1. The hotel environment is great! It's almost a park-like environment, with a beautiful lake and black swans swimming around.
2. The hotel has multiple outdoor forest hot springs, as well as indoor bathing pools and swimming pools. This hot spring area should be independently operated to the outside world. It is free for hotel guests, but it should have been open for a long time and is a bit old.
3. The hotel's breakfast is very good, with many varieties, Chinese and Western buffet, and the noodles taste particularly good!
4. The hot water in the room is particularly good, the water is large and the temperature is high! Bathing is very comfortable! Soaking in the bathtub in the room is also very nice!
5. The service is very good. When I checked in, I added the contact information of the housekeeper Mei Xiaohan. If I have any questions, I can provide feedback at any time.
6. Mineral water is provided free of charge and in unlimited quantities.

Several areas for improvement:
1. The lighting in the room is too dim, making people feel depressed and drowsy. This should be improved by replacing the light bulb with a larger wattage. For example, changing the bedside lamp to a spotlight bulb can also be better. (There is also a broken light bulb in the room)
2. The door of the room where you checked in was not closed tightly, resulting in poor sound insulation. If someone spoke at the door or next door, you could hear clearly.

The cost of the above two improvements should not be high. If they are upgraded, the hotel will be even more perfect! I will definitely choose this hotel next time I come to Emeishan!

[Traffic] The hotel is located in Hongzhu Mountain Scenic Area, about 10 minutes' drive from Emeishan High-speed Railway Station. The hotel provides free pick-up service, but the station must be Emeishan instead of Emei. Friends who come by high-speed rail must pay attention~
The hotel is built on the mountain, with a total of 8 buildings connected by Shangshan Road. The main building is Building No. 5, which was originally scheduled, but it became Building No. 8 after the itinerary was changed. Building No. 8 is located at the highest and deepest point. Although the hotel provides an internal shuttle bus, the traffic is still a little inconvenient. You have to go to the hot spring clubhouse to soak in the hot springs, and you have to go to building No. 7 for meals. We are embarrassed to trouble others to send a car, and we basically come here on our own.
[Room facilities] It belongs to an old-fashioned hotel. Although the facilities are complete, they are old, especially the TV, which is small and inconvenient to cast a screen. It is not very friendly to young people like us, but it does not affect normal accommodation and use.
[Service] The service is really very good, absolutely five-star, basically not too much to respond to requests, the pick-up station and the shuttle bus will respond relatively quickly and there will be a dedicated person in charge. Tang Jun, who picked up the station, was very enthusiastic and serious. He introduced the hotel's facilities and services in detail, and also provided various suggestions for surrounding tours and eating and drinking. He would also remind the weather every morning and ask about the arrangement of the pick-up station in advance. He was attentive and thoughtful. Must like!
[Value for money] It should be considered very high, recommended~
Generally speaking, it is very good. I will definitely bring my parents here in the future. It is very suitable for the whole family to relax and vacation~
